But according to the bug report, this doesn't work on the Acer TravelMate 5735Z.\n\nThe fix is to add the Acer TravelMate 5735Z to the DMI table in video_detect.c with a callback to force_native, so {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01RaEqpVWn8KfK4h9MwuAkcT","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"thinking","thinking":"Now I understand the issue. The ACPI video backlight driver calls acpi_video_init_brightness, which calls acpi_video_get_levels to get the brightness levels.
